# Individual Student Profiles

<div class="grid cards" markdown style="text-align: center;">

[‚Üê Overview](../){ .md-button }
[Reading Analysis](../reading_analysis/){ .md-button }
[Campus Breakdown](../campus_breakdown/){ .md-button }

</div>

This comprehensive directory provides detailed performance profiles for all 423 students with Reading data, organized by risk level based on Fall-to-Winter 2025 Growth X scores. Each profile includes subject-specific performance metrics, intelligent cross-subject analysis, and targeted action recommendations.

## Understanding Growth X

**Growth X** represents how many times the typical student growth a student has achieved. For example:
- Growth X of 2 = twice the typical growth
- Growth X of 1 = typical expected growth
- Growth X of 0 = no growth
- Growth X of -1 = regression equivalent to typical growth amount

## Risk Level System

Students are categorized into five risk levels based on their **Combined Score** (sum of highest Reading/Science Growth X scores):

| Risk Level | Growth X Range | Definition | Action Timeline |
|------------|----------------|------------|-----------------|
| Critical Risk | < -5 | Significant regression requiring immediate intervention | **Emergency** - Within 24-48 hours |
| High Risk | -5 to 0 | Below-target growth needing urgent support | **Urgent** - Within 1 week |
| Moderate Risk | 0 to 5 | Some growth but below optimal trajectory | **Important** - Within 2-3 weeks |
| Low Risk | 5 to 10 | Good progress approaching targets | **Monitor** - Ongoing support |
| Exceeding | > 10 | Exceptional growth exceeding expectations | **Celebrate** - Enrichment opportunities |

## Complete Student Directory

All 423 students with Reading data are listed below alphabetically. Click to expand each student's detailed profile.

??? success "A'Leiah Jenkins - Low Risk (1.75)"

    **Campus:** Nova Academy Austin | **Level:** L1 | **Age Grade:** 2

    ### Performance Overview

    | Subject | Growth X | HMG | RIT Fall '25 | RIT Winter '25 | Course(s) |
    |---------|----------|-----|--------------|----------------|-----------|
    | Science | No data available | No data available | No data available | No data available | No data available |
    | Reading | 1.8 | No data available | 169 | 183 | Amplify, ClearFluency Grade 1, Lexia Core5 |
    | Math | No data available | No data available | No data available | No data available | No data available |
    | Language | No data available | No data available | No data available | No data available | No data available |

    ### Analysis

    **Issues Identified:**

    - Moderate growth with room for acceleration

    **Cross-Subject Inference:**

    - Continue monitoring progress and adjust interventions based on ongoing assessment data

    ### Recommended Actions

    **Immediate (Week 1-2):**

    - Acknowledge positive progress and growth mindset
    - Identify any remaining skill gaps for fine-tuning

    **Short-term (Weeks 3-6):**

    - Provide enrichment opportunities to deepen understanding
    - Encourage leadership roles in collaborative learning
    - Maintain current support structures and momentum
    - Monitor to ensure consistent progress continues

    **Long-term (Quarter):**

    - Prepare for advanced coursework or acceleration opportunities
    - Foster peer tutoring or mentorship roles
    - Build critical thinking and application skills
    - Maintain regular progress monitoring to sustain growth


??? tip "Abi Constain - Exceeding (14)"

    **Campus:** Alpha School Miami | **Level:** MS | **Age Grade:** 8

    ### Performance Overview

    | Subject | Growth X | HMG | RIT Fall '25 | RIT Winter '25 | Course(s) |
    |---------|----------|-----|--------------|----------------|-----------|
    | Science | 5.0 | 3 | 219 | 224 | Science Hole-filling (G4) - MobyMax |
    | Reading | 9.0 | 6 | 225 | 234 | Core Knowledge Reading Grade 6/6, Core Knowledge Reading Grade 7/7 |
    | Math | -1.5 | 2 | 225 | 219 | Edia G3 Hole-filling |
    | Language | 4.0 | 4 | 222 | 226 | [Freckle] Language G5 hole-filling, MobyMax - Language 5 Hole-Filling |

    ### Analysis

    **Issues Identified:**

    - Negative growth in: Math
    - Highly uneven growth across subjects

    **Cross-Subject Inference:**

    - Strong performance across most subjects except Math - may indicate course difficulty mismatch or need for targeted support
    - Large variance in growth suggests engagement or placement inconsistencies - review course alignment

    ### Recommended Actions

    **Immediate (Week 1-2):**

    - Celebrate exceptional growth and achievement
    - Explore opportunities for advanced or accelerated coursework

    **Short-term (Weeks 3-6):**

    - Provide enrichment projects and independent study options
    - Consider leadership or peer teaching opportunities
    - Introduce complex, real-world application tasks
    - Maintain challenge level to sustain engagement

    **Long-term (Quarter):**

    - Plan pathway for continued advanced learning
    - Develop student as model and mentor for peers
    - Explore extracurricular academic opportunities
    - Maintain monitoring to ensure sustained excellence

??? danger "Adrienne Laswell - Critical Risk (-9)"

    **Campus:** Alpha High School | **Level:** HS | **Age Grade:** 9

    ### Performance Overview

    | Subject | Growth X | HMG | RIT Fall '25 | RIT Winter '25 | Course(s) |
    |---------|----------|-----|--------------|----------------|-----------|
    | Science | -1.0 | No data available | 241 | 240 | Edmentum - Biology |
    | Reading | -8.0 | 7 | 256 | 248 | Reading G11 Hole-Filling - 100 for 100, Reading SAT Level 3 |
    | Math | 14.0 | No data available | 263 | 277 | Math Academy - SAT Math Fundamentals |
    | Language | 7.0 | No data available | 250 | 257 | MobyMax - Language 8 Hole-Filling |

    ### Analysis

    **Issues Identified:**

    - Negative growth in: Reading, Science
    - Highly uneven growth across subjects

    **Cross-Subject Inference:**

    - Strong Math but weak Science suggests vocabulary or science-specific conceptual challenges
    - Strong Language but weak Reading suggests stamina issues or difficulty with complex texts
    - Large variance in growth suggests engagement or placement inconsistencies - review course alignment

    ### Recommended Actions

    **Immediate (Week 1-2):**

    - Schedule emergency intervention meeting with student, parents, and support team
    - Conduct diagnostic assessment to identify specific skill gaps
    - Implement daily 1-on-1 tutoring sessions (minimum 30 minutes)
    - Review course placement and consider immediate adjustments

    **Short-term (Weeks 3-6):**

    - Develop individualized learning plan with measurable weekly goals
    - Increase progress monitoring to twice weekly
    - Connect with subject-area specialist for targeted intervention
    - Consider peer tutoring or study group participation

    **Long-term (Quarter):**

    - Establish ongoing case management with regular check-ins
    - Build foundational skills through systematic remediation
    - Monitor for social-emotional factors impacting learning
    - Plan for extended learning opportunities (summer, after-school)


??? warning "Aheli Shah - High Risk (7)"

    **Campus:** Alpha High School | **Level:** HS | **Age Grade:** 9

    ### Performance Overview

    | Subject | Growth X | HMG | RIT Fall '25 | RIT Winter '25 | Course(s) |
    |---------|----------|-----|--------------|----------------|-----------|
    | Science | 9.0 | 8 | 224 | 233 | Edmentum - Biology |
    | Reading | -2.0 | 9 | 238 | 236 | Grade 10 Reading |
    | Math | 4.0 | No data available | 252 | 256 | Math Academy - SAT Math Fundamentals |
    | Language | -6.0 | No data available | 241 | 235 | eGumpp |

    ### Analysis

    **Issues Identified:**

    - Negative growth in: Reading, Language
    - Highly uneven growth across subjects

    **Cross-Subject Inference:**

    - Large variance in growth suggests engagement or placement inconsistencies - review course alignment

    ### Recommended Actions

    **Immediate (Week 1-2):**

    - Meet with student to discuss performance and identify barriers
    - Review recent assessment data and identify priority skill areas
    - Adjust seating/grouping for increased teacher proximity and support

    **Short-term (Weeks 3-6):**

    - Implement targeted small-group instruction 3x weekly
    - Increase formative assessment frequency to track progress
    - Provide scaffolded learning materials and structured practice
    - Coordinate with family on home support strategies

    **Long-term (Quarter):**

    - Monitor progress bi-weekly and adjust interventions as needed
    - Build student self-advocacy and metacognitive skills
    - Consider additional support services if progress plateaus
    - Track engagement and motivation alongside academic metrics

    **Campus:** NextGen Academy | **Level:** L2 | **Age Grade:** 5

    ### Performance Overview

    | Subject | Growth X | HMG | RIT Fall '25 | RIT Winter '25 | Course(s) |
    |---------|----------|-----|--------------|----------------|-----------|
    | Science | 4.3 | 3 | 209 | 222 | MobyMax - Science G4 |
    | Reading | -2.0 | 2 | 221 | 219 | Core Knowledge Reading Grade 3/3 |
    | Math | 1.3 | 2 | 206 | 215 | Zearn - Grade 3 |
    | Language | -12.0 | 4 | 218 | 206 | MobyMax - Language 5 |

    ### Analysis

    **Issues Identified:**

    - Negative growth in: Reading, Language
    - Highly uneven growth across subjects

    **Cross-Subject Inference:**

    - Large variance in growth suggests engagement or placement inconsistencies - review course alignment

    ### Recommended Actions

    **Immediate (Week 1-2):**

    - Meet with student to discuss performance and identify barriers
    - Review recent assessment data and identify priority skill areas
    - Adjust seating/grouping for increased teacher proximity and support

    **Short-term (Weeks 3-6):**

    - Implement targeted small-group instruction 3x weekly
    - Increase formative assessment frequency to track progress
    - Provide scaffolded learning materials and structured practice
    - Coordinate with family on home support strategies

    **Long-term (Quarter):**

    - Monitor progress bi-weekly and adjust interventions as needed
    - Build student self-advocacy and metacognitive skills
    - Consider additional support services if progress plateaus
    - Track engagement and motivation alongside academic metrics

??? danger "Ben De Amorim - Critical Risk (1)"

    **Campus:** Alpha School Miami | **Level:** MS | **Age Grade:** 6

    ### Performance Overview

    | Subject | Growth X | HMG | RIT Fall '25 | RIT Winter '25 | Course(s) |
    |---------|----------|-----|--------------|----------------|-----------|
    | Science | -7.0 | 4 | 225 | 218 | Science Hole-filling (G5) - MobyMax |
    | Reading | 8.0 | 7 | 218 | 226 | Core Knowledge Reading Grade 8/8 |
    | Math | 0.3 | 5 | 225 | 227 | Math Academy - Prealgebra |
    | Language | -1.0 | 6 | 226 | 225 | [Freckle] Language G7 hole-filling, MobyMax - Language 7 Hole-Filling |

    ### Analysis

    **Issues Identified:**

    - Negative growth in: Science, Language
    - Highly uneven growth across subjects

    **Cross-Subject Inference:**

    - Strong Reading but weak Language suggests grammar/mechanics gaps despite comprehension strength
    - Large variance in growth suggests engagement or placement inconsistencies - review course alignment

    ### Recommended Actions

    **Immediate (Week 1-2):**

    - Schedule emergency intervention meeting with student, parents, and support team
    - Conduct diagnostic assessment to identify specific skill gaps
    - Implement daily 1-on-1 tutoring sessions (minimum 30 minutes)
    - Review course placement and consider immediate adjustments

    **Short-term (Weeks 3-6):**

    - Develop individualized learning plan with measurable weekly goals
    - Increase progress monitoring to twice weekly
    - Connect with subject-area specialist for targeted intervention
    - Consider peer tutoring or study group participation

    **Long-term (Quarter):**

    - Establish ongoing case management with regular check-ins
    - Build foundational skills through systematic remediation
    - Monitor for social-emotional factors impacting learning
    - Plan for extended learning opportunities (summer, after-school)

    - Schedule emergency intervention meeting with student, parents, and support team

    - Implement daily 1-on-1 tutoring sessions (minimum 30 minutes)
    - Review course placement and consider immediate adjustments

    **Short-term (Weeks 3-6):**

    - Develop individualized learning plan with measurable weekly goals
    - Increase progress monitoring to twice weekly
    - Connect with subject-area specialist for targeted intervention
    - Consider peer tutoring or study group participation

    **Long-term (Quarter):**

    - Establish ongoing case management with regular check-ins
    - Build foundational skills through systematic remediation
    - Monitor for social-emotional factors impacting learning
    - Plan for extended learning opportunities (summer, after-school)

    **Cross-Subject Inference:**

    - Build foundational skills through systematic remediation
    - Monitor for social-emotional factors impacting learning

    **Campus:** Alpha High School | **Level:** HS | **Age Grade:** 9

    ### Performance Overview

    | Subject | Growth X | HMG | RIT Fall '25 | RIT Winter '25 | Course(s) |
    |---------|----------|-----|--------------|----------------|-----------|
    | Science | -5.0 | 9 | 228 | 223 | Edmentum - AP Biology |
    | Reading | -6.0 | 12 | 238 | 232 | Reading SAT Level 3 |
    | Math | 6.0 | 8 | 258 | 264 | Math Academy - Integrated Math I (Honors) |
    | Language | 4.0 | 8 | 229 | 233 | eGumpp |

    ### Analysis

    **Issues Identified:**

    - Negative growth in: Reading, Science
    - Highly uneven growth across subjects

    **Cross-Subject Inference:**

    - Strong Math but weak Science suggests vocabulary or science-specific conceptual challenges
    - Large variance in growth suggests engagement or placement inconsistencies - review course alignment

    ### Recommended Actions

    **Immediate (Week 1-2):**

    - Schedule emergency intervention meeting with student, parents, and support team
    - Conduct diagnostic assessment to identify specific skill gaps
    - Implement daily 1-on-1 tutoring sessions (minimum 30 minutes)
    - Review course placement and consider immediate adjustments

    **Short-term (Weeks 3-6):**

    - Develop individualized learning plan with measurable weekly goals
    - Increase progress monitoring to twice weekly
    - Connect with subject-area specialist for targeted intervention
    - Consider peer tutoring or study group participation

    **Long-term (Quarter):**

    - Establish ongoing case management with regular check-ins
    - Build foundational skills through systematic remediation
    - Monitor for social-emotional factors impacting learning
    - Plan for extended learning opportunities (summer, after-school)

    - Strong performance across most subjects except Reading - may indicate course difficulty mismatch or need for targeted support

    - Implement targeted small-group instruction 3x weekly
    - Increase formative assessment frequency to track progress
    - Provide scaffolded learning materials and structured practice
    - Coordinate with family on home support strategies

    **Long-term (Quarter):**

    - Monitor progress bi-weekly and adjust interventions as needed
    - Build student self-advocacy and metacognitive skills
    - Consider additional support services if progress plateaus
    - Track engagement and motivation alongside academic metrics

    **Campus:** Alpha High School | **Level:** HS | **Age Grade:** 10

    ### Performance Overview

    | Subject | Growth X | HMG | RIT Fall '25 | RIT Winter '25 | Course(s) |
    |---------|----------|-----|--------------|----------------|-----------|
    | Science | -8.0 | No data available | 268 | 260 | AP Computer Science A with Runestone, Edmentum - Chemistry, PhysicsGraph |
    | Reading | -1.0 | 7 | 257 | 256 | Reading SAT Level 4 |
    | Math | 5.0 | No data available | 283 | 288 | Math Academy - SAT Math Fundamentals |
    | Language | 7.0 | 8 | 256 | 263 | No data available |

    ### Analysis

    **Issues Identified:**

    - Negative growth in: Reading, Science
    - Highly uneven growth across subjects

    **Cross-Subject Inference:**

    - Strong Language but weak Reading suggests stamina issues or difficulty with complex texts
    - Large variance in growth suggests engagement or placement inconsistencies - review course alignment

    ### Recommended Actions

    **Immediate (Week 1-2):**

    - Schedule emergency intervention meeting with student, parents, and support team
    - Conduct diagnostic assessment to identify specific skill gaps
    - Implement daily 1-on-1 tutoring sessions (minimum 30 minutes)
    - Review course placement and consider immediate adjustments

    **Short-term (Weeks 3-6):**

    - Develop individualized learning plan with measurable weekly goals
    - Increase progress monitoring to twice weekly

??? danger "Ju Orloff - Critical Risk (-7)"

    **Campus:** Alpha School Miami | **Level:** HS | **Age Grade:** 10

    ### Performance Overview

    | Subject | Growth X | HMG | RIT Fall '25 | RIT Winter '25 | Course(s) |
    |---------|----------|-----|--------------|----------------|-----------|
    | Science | 1.0 | 9 | 201 | 205 | Edmentum - AP Biology |
    | Reading | -8.0 | 10 | 224 | 216 | 100 for 100, Grade 11 Reading |
    | Math | -0.8 | 8 | 221 | 218 | Math Academy - SAT Math Fundamentals |
    | Language | 7.0 | 8 | 233 | 240 | eGumpp |

    ### Analysis

    **Issues Identified:**

    - Negative growth in: Reading, Math
    - Highly uneven growth across subjects

    **Cross-Subject Inference:**

    - Strong Language but weak Reading suggests stamina issues or difficulty with complex texts
    - Large variance in growth suggests engagement or placement inconsistencies - review course alignment

    ### Recommended Actions

    **Immediate (Week 1-2):**

    - Schedule emergency intervention meeting with student, parents, and support team
    - Conduct diagnostic assessment to identify specific skill gaps
    - Implement daily 1-on-1 tutoring sessions (minimum 30 minutes)
    - Review course placement and consider immediate adjustments

    **Short-term (Weeks 3-6):**

    - Develop individualized learning plan with measurable weekly goals
    - Increase progress monitoring to twice weekly
    - Connect with subject-area specialist for targeted intervention
    - Consider peer tutoring or study group participation

    **Long-term (Quarter):**

    - Establish ongoing case management with regular check-ins
    - Build foundational skills through systematic remediation
    - Monitor for social-emotional factors impacting learning
    - Plan for extended learning opportunities (summer, after-school)

??? danger "Kavin Lingham - Critical Risk (-5)"

    **Campus:** Alpha High School | **Level:** HS | **Age Grade:** 10

    ### Performance Overview

    | Subject | Growth X | HMG | RIT Fall '25 | RIT Winter '25 | Course(s) |
    |---------|----------|-----|--------------|----------------|-----------|
    | Science | -9.0 | No data available | 262 | 253 | Edmentum - Chemistry |
    | Reading | 4.0 | 10 | 239 | 243 | No data available |
    | Math | 2.0 | 8 | 268 | 270 | Math Academy - SAT Math Fundamentals |
    | Language | 10.0 | 8 | 232 | 242 | MobyMax  - Language 9 Hole-filling |

    ### Analysis

    **Issues Identified:**

    - Negative growth in: Science
    - Highly uneven growth across subjects

    **Cross-Subject Inference:**

    - Large variance in growth suggests engagement or placement inconsistencies - review course alignment

    ### Recommended Actions

    **Immediate (Week 1-2):**

    - Schedule emergency intervention meeting with student, parents, and support team
    - Conduct diagnostic assessment to identify specific skill gaps
    - Implement daily 1-on-1 tutoring sessions (minimum 30 minutes)
    - Review course placement and consider immediate adjustments

    **Short-term (Weeks 3-6):**

    - Develop individualized learning plan with measurable weekly goals
    - Increase progress monitoring to twice weekly
    - Connect with subject-area specialist for targeted intervention
    - Consider peer tutoring or study group participation

    **Long-term (Quarter):**

    - Establish ongoing case management with regular check-ins
    - Build foundational skills through systematic remediation
    - Monitor for social-emotional factors impacting learning
    - Plan for extended learning opportunities (summer, after-school)

    | Math | 17.0 | 8 | 265 | 282 | Math Academy - SAT Math Fundamentals |
    | Language | 2.0 | 9 | 253 | 255 | AP Language and Composition |

    ### Analysis

    **Issues Identified:**

    - Negative growth in: Reading
    - Highly uneven growth across subjects

    **Cross-Subject Inference:**

    - Large variance in growth suggests engagement or placement inconsistencies - review course alignment

    ### Recommended Actions

    **Immediate (Week 1-2):**

    - Schedule emergency intervention meeting with student, parents, and support team
    - Conduct diagnostic assessment to identify specific skill gaps
    - Implement daily 1-on-1 tutoring sessions (minimum 30 minutes)
    - Review course placement and consider immediate adjustments

    **Short-term (Weeks 3-6):**

    - Develop individualized learning plan with measurable weekly goals
    - Increase progress monitoring to twice weekly
    - Connect with subject-area specialist for targeted intervention
    - Consider peer tutoring or study group participation

    **Long-term (Quarter):**

    - Establish ongoing case management with regular check-ins
    - Build foundational skills through systematic remediation
    - Monitor for social-emotional factors impacting learning
    - Plan for extended learning opportunities (summer, after-school)

    | Math | 2.0 | 8 | 260 | 262 | Math Academy - SAT Math Fundamentals |
    | Language | 3.0 | 8 | 239 | 242 | eGumpp, MobyMax - Language 6, MobyMax - Language 8 Hole-Filling |

    ### Analysis

    **Issues Identified:**

    - Negative growth in: Reading, Science
    - Highly uneven growth across subjects

    **Cross-Subject Inference:**

    - Large variance in growth suggests engagement or placement inconsistencies - review course alignment

    ### Recommended Actions

    **Immediate (Week 1-2):**

    - Schedule emergency intervention meeting with student, parents, and support team
    - Conduct diagnostic assessment to identify specific skill gaps
    - Implement daily 1-on-1 tutoring sessions (minimum 30 minutes)
    - Review course placement and consider immediate adjustments

    **Short-term (Weeks 3-6):**

    - Develop individualized learning plan with measurable weekly goals
    - Increase progress monitoring to twice weekly
    - Connect with subject-area specialist for targeted intervention
    - Consider peer tutoring or study group participation

    **Long-term (Quarter):**

    - Establish ongoing case management with regular check-ins
    - Build foundational skills through systematic remediation
    - Monitor for social-emotional factors impacting learning
    - Plan for extended learning opportunities (summer, after-school)

    **Campus:** Alpha School Austin | **Level:** MS | **Age Grade:** 8

    | Subject | Growth X | HMG | RIT Fall '25 | RIT Winter '25 | Course(s) |
    |---------|----------|-----|--------------|----------------|-----------|

    | Reading | -1.0 | No data available | 235 | 234 | MobyMax - Reading Skills Literature 8 Hole-Filling |
    | Math | 3.7 | 8 | 253 | 264 | Math Academy - Integrated Math I (Honors) |
    | Language | 6.0 | No data available | 226 | 232 | eGumpp, MobyMax - Language 8 Hole-Filling |

    ### Analysis

    **Issues Identified:**

    - Negative growth in: Reading, Science
    - Highly uneven growth across subjects

    **Cross-Subject Inference:**

    - Strong Language but weak Reading suggests stamina issues or difficulty with complex texts
    - Large variance in growth suggests engagement or placement inconsistencies - review course alignment

    ### Recommended Actions

    **Immediate (Week 1-2):**

    - Schedule emergency intervention meeting with student, parents, and support team
    - Conduct diagnostic assessment to identify specific skill gaps
    - Implement daily 1-on-1 tutoring sessions (minimum 30 minutes)
    - Review course placement and consider immediate adjustments

    **Short-term (Weeks 3-6):**

    - Develop individualized learning plan with measurable weekly goals
    - Increase progress monitoring to twice weekly
    - Connect with subject-area specialist for targeted intervention
    - Consider peer tutoring or study group participation

    **Long-term (Quarter):**

    - Establish ongoing case management with regular check-ins
    - Build foundational skills through systematic remediation
    - Monitor for social-emotional factors impacting learning
    - Plan for extended learning opportunities (summer, after-school)

??? danger "Stella Cole - Critical Risk (-7)"

    **Campus:** Alpha High School | **Level:** HS | **Age Grade:** 10

    ### Performance Overview

    | Subject | Growth X | HMG | RIT Fall '25 | RIT Winter '25 | Course(s) |
    |---------|----------|-----|--------------|----------------|-----------|
    | Science | -3.0 | 8 | 227 | 224 | Edmentum - Chemistry |
    | Reading | -4.0 | 10 | 248 | 244 | Reading Grade 11 Hole-Filling - Stella Cole, Reading SAT Level 3 |
    | Math | 5.0 | 8 | 257 | 262 | Math Academy - Algebra I |
    | Language | 13.0 | 8 | 246 | 259 | eGumpp |

    ### Analysis

    **Issues Identified:**

    - Negative growth in: Reading, Science
    - Highly uneven growth across subjects

    **Cross-Subject Inference:**

    - Strong Language but weak Reading suggests stamina issues or difficulty with complex texts
    - Large variance in growth suggests engagement or placement inconsistencies - review course alignment

    ### Recommended Actions

    **Immediate (Week 1-2):**

    - Schedule emergency intervention meeting with student, parents, and support team
    - Conduct diagnostic assessment to identify specific skill gaps
    - Implement daily 1-on-1 tutoring sessions (minimum 30 minutes)
    - Review course placement and consider immediate adjustments

    **Short-term (Weeks 3-6):**

    - Develop individualized learning plan with measurable weekly goals
    - Increase progress monitoring to twice weekly
    - Connect with subject-area specialist for targeted intervention
    - Consider peer tutoring or study group participation

    **Long-term (Quarter):**

    - Establish ongoing case management with regular check-ins
    - Build foundational skills through systematic remediation
    - Monitor for social-emotional factors impacting learning
    - Plan for extended learning opportunities (summer, after-school)

    - Increase progress monitoring to twice weekly
    - Connect with subject-area specialist for targeted intervention
    - Consider peer tutoring or study group participation

    **Long-term (Quarter):**

    - Establish ongoing case management with regular check-ins
    - Build foundational skills through systematic remediation
    - Monitor for social-emotional factors impacting learning
    - Plan for extended learning opportunities (summer, after-school)
